                   EstimateRAWSetup.TESTFIELD("Paragraph No.(ExecutionCost)");  //DP01485
                   EstimateRAWSetup.TESTFIELD("Paragraph No.(GeneralCost)");
                   EstimateRAWSetup.TESTFIELD("Paragraph No.(Profit/Risk)");

    { 1100525005;;DataItem;                  ;
               DataItemTable=Table11012265;
               DataItemTableView=SORTING(Project No.,Principal,No.);
               OnAfterGetRecord=BEGIN

                                  ProjectPrincipal.GET("Project No.", Principal);
                                  ProjectPrincipal.CALCFIELDS("Principal Name");

                                  TotalAmount := 0;
                                  PrintTotal := FALSE;

                                  SubtotalAmount := 0;

                                  CALCFIELDS("First Motivation Description", "Last Motivation Description", "First Motivation Period", "Last Motivation Period");  //DP01491

    { 1100525006;2;DataItem;                 ;
               DataItemTable=Table11012266;
               DataItemTableView=SORTING(Project No.,Principal,Installment Overview,Tender Paragraph No.,Entry Type)
                                 WHERE(Entry Type=FILTER(Normal));
               OnPreDataItem=BEGIN
                               IF PageLoop.Number <> 1 THEN
                                 CurrReport.BREAK;
                             END;

               OnAfterGetRecord=BEGIN
                                  CALCFIELDS(Description, "Element Quantity", Unit, "Unit Price (FCY)", Layout);

    { 1100525054;3;DataItem;Subtotal         ;
               DataItemTable=Table2000000026;
               DataItemTableView=SORTING(Number)
                                 WHERE(Number=CONST(1));
               OnPreDataItem=VAR
                               InstallmentOverviewLine@1100525000 : Record 11012266;
                               PrintSubtotal@1100525001 : Boolean;
                             BEGIN
                               //print SubTotal on first TenderParagraph of Summary
                               IF NOT SubtotalPrinted THEN BEGIN
                                 InstallmentOverviewLine.COPY("Installment Overview Line");
                                 IF InstallmentOverviewLine.NEXT <> 0 THEN BEGIN
                                   IF COPYSTR(InstallmentOverviewLine."Tender Paragraph No.", 1, 1) = '9' THEN BEGIN
                                     SubtotalAmount := TotalAmount;
                                     PrintSubtotal := TRUE;
                                   END;
                                 END;
                               END;

                               IF COPYSTR("Installment Overview Line"."Tender Paragraph No.", 1, 1) = '9' THEN BEGIN
                                 IF PrintSubtotal AND NOT SubtotalPrinted THEN
                                   SubtotalPrinted := TRUE;
                               END;

                               IF NOT PrintSubtotal THEN
                                 CurrReport.BREAK;

                               IF SubtotalPrinted THEN
                                 PrintSubtotal := FALSE
                               ELSE
                                 CurrReport.BREAK;
                             END;
                              }

    { 1100525055;4;Column;Number_Subtotal    ;
               SourceExpr=Number }

    { 1100525053;4;Column;SubTotalAmount_Subtotal;
               SourceExpr=SubtotalAmount }

    { 1100525007;2;DataItem;Excess           ;
               DataItemTable=Table11012266;
               DataItemTableView=SORTING(Project No.,Principal,Installment Overview,Tender Paragraph No.,Entry Type)
                                 WHERE(Entry Type=CONST(Excess));
               OnPreDataItem=BEGIN
                               IF PageLoop.Number <> 1 THEN
                                 CurrReport.BREAK;
                             END;

               OnAfterGetRecord=BEGIN
                                  CALCFIELDS(Description, "Element Quantity", Unit, "Settlement Price (FCY)", "Settlement Type");

                                  IF ("Element Quantity" = 0) AND ("Settlement Type" = "Settlement Type"::"Non Settling") THEN
                                    CurrReport.SKIP;

                                  SetText(Excess);

                                  IF "Settlement Type" = "Settlement Type"::"Non Settling" THEN BEGIN
                                    "Settlement Price (FCY)" := 0;
                                    "Production Value Cum. (FCY)" := 0;
                                  END;

                                  TotalAmount += "Production Value Cum. (FCY)";
                                END;

               DataItemLinkReference=Installment Overview;
               DataItemLink=Project No.=FIELD(Project No.),
                            Principal=FIELD(Principal),
                            Installment Overview=FIELD(No.) }

      DeclaredDec@1100409003 : Decimal;
      Vatpart@1100409001 : Decimal;
      Text000@1100409004 : TextConst 'DEU=%1 - %2;ENU=%1 - %2;NLD=%1 - %2;NOR=%1 - %2;SVE=%1 - %2';

    LOCAL PROCEDURE GetReportName@1100525003() : Text;
    BEGIN
      EXIT(DELSTR(CurrReport.OBJECTID, 1, STRPOS(CurrReport.OBJECTID, ' ')));
    END;

    PROCEDURE SetText@1100525000(InstallmentOverviewLine@1100525000 : Record 11012266);
    BEGIN
      InstallmentOverviewLine.CALCFIELDS(Finished, "Settlement Type");
      IF InstallmentOverviewLine.Finished THEN
        FinishedText := 'G'
      ELSE
        FinishedText := '';

      CASE InstallmentOverviewLine."Settlement Type" OF
        InstallmentOverviewLine."Settlement Type"::"Non Settling": SettlementTypeText := 'N';
        InstallmentOverviewLine."Settlement Type"::Settling: SettlementTypeText := 'V';
        InstallmentOverviewLine."Settlement Type"::Approved: SettlementTypeText := 'A';
        InstallmentOverviewLine."Settlement Type"::Reduction: SettlementTypeText := 'M';
        InstallmentOverviewLine."Settlement Type"::Open: SettlementTypeText := 'O';
      ELSE
        SettlementTypeText := '';
      END;
    END;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE CalculateDeclared@1100525001() : Decimal;
    VAR
      InstallmentMotivation@1100525002 : Record 11012471;
      InstallmentMotivationLine@1100525001 : Record 11012472;
      InstallmentOverview@1100525003 : Record 11012265;
      InstallmentOverviewLine@1100525000 : Record 11012266;
    BEGIN
      //C041302.sn
      DeclaredDec := 0;
      InstallmentOverview.SETRANGE("Project No.", "Installment Overview"."Project No.");
      InstallmentOverview.SETRANGE(Principal, "Installment Overview".Principal);
      InstallmentOverview.SETFILTER("No.", '<%1', "Installment Overview"."No.");
      IF NOT InstallmentOverview.FINDLAST THEN
        EXIT(DeclaredDec);
      //C041302.en
      //
      WITH InstallmentOverview DO BEGIN
        InstallmentMotivation.SETRANGE("Project No.", "Project No.");
        InstallmentMotivation.SETRANGE(Principal, Principal);
        InstallmentMotivation.SETRANGE("Production Date", "First Motivation Date", "Last Motivation Date");
        InstallmentMotivation.SETRANGE(Status, InstallmentMotivation.Status::Approved);
        IF InstallmentMotivation.FINDLAST THEN BEGIN  //C041302: last motivation contains cumulative total for previous period
          InstallmentMotivationLine.SETRANGE("Project No.", InstallmentMotivation."Project No.");
          InstallmentMotivationLine.SETRANGE(Principal, InstallmentMotivation.Principal);
          InstallmentMotivationLine.SETRANGE("Production Date", InstallmentMotivation."Production Date");
          IF InstallmentMotivationLine.FINDSET THEN BEGIN
            REPEAT
              DeclaredDec +=
                InstallmentMotivationLine."Production Value Cum. (FCY)" +
                InstallmentMotivationLine."Excess Prod. Value Cum. (FCY)";
            UNTIL InstallmentMotivationLine.NEXT = 0;
          END;
          //
          InstallmentOverviewLine.SETRANGE("Project No.", InstallmentMotivation."Project No.");
          InstallmentOverviewLine.SETRANGE(Principal, InstallmentMotivation.Principal);
          InstallmentOverviewLine.SETRANGE("Installment Overview", "No.");
          InstallmentOverviewLine.SETFILTER("Tender Paragraph No.",'%1|%2|%3',
            EstimateRAWSetup."Paragraph No.(ExecutionCost)",
            EstimateRAWSetup."Paragraph No.(GeneralCost)",
            EstimateRAWSetup."Paragraph No.(Profit/Risk)");
          IF InstallmentOverviewLine.FINDSET THEN BEGIN
            REPEAT
              DeclaredDec += InstallmentOverviewLine."Production Value Cum. (FCY)";
            UNTIL InstallmentOverviewLine.NEXT = 0;
          END;
        END;
      END;
      //
      EXIT(DeclaredDec);
    END;

    BEGIN
    {
      DP01491: fill weekcode (Overview Period: 4week period from StartDateInvoice) and weeknumber (calendarweek: based on start/end ProductionDate)
    }
    END.
  }

  <Code>Public Function BlankZero(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    If Value = 0 Then
        Return ""
    End If
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankPos(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    If Value &gt; 0 Then
        Return ""
    End If
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankZeroAndPos(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    If Value &gt;= 0 Then
        Return ""
    End If
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankNeg(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    If Value &lt; 0 Then
        Return ""
    End If
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankNegAndZero(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    If Value &lt;= 0 Then
        Return ""
    End If
    Return Value
End Function

Shared offset As Integer
Shared newgroup As Object
Shared currentgroup1 As Object
Shared currentgroup2 As Object

Public Function GetGroupPageNumber(newgroup2 As Boolean, pagenumber As Integer) As Object
    If newgroup2
        offset = pagenumber - 1
    End If
    Return pagenumber - offset
End Function

Public Function InNewGroup(group1 As Object, group2 As Object) As Boolean
    newgroup = False
    If Not (group1 = currentgroup1)
        newgroup = True
        currentgroup2 = group2
        currentgroup1 = group1
    Else
        If Not (group2 = currentgroup2)
            newgroup = True
            currentgroup2 = group2
        End If
    End If
    Return newgroup
End Function

Shared Data1 As Object

Public Function GetData(Num As Integer) As Object
    Return Cstr(Choose(Num, Split(Cstr(Data1), Chr(177))))
End Function

Public Function SetData(NewData As Object)
    If NewData &lt;&gt; "" Then
        Data1 = NewData
    End If
End Function
</Code>

  <ConsumeContainerWhitespace>true</ConsumeContainerWhitespace>
  <rd:ReportUnitType>Cm</rd:ReportUnitType>
</Report>
    END_OF_RDLDATA
